Hindu physiologists fancy that the mind de- scends from its seat in the forehead to its other seats, the neck, breast, umbilicus and <i>terminus rectum.</i> (<tam>தத்துவக்</tam>. <tam>சிவ</tam>. <tam>சி</tam>.)</p2> <p2><tam>கீழிருக்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To lie under, to be under one's dominion or control.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழாறு</tam>, <i>s.</i> A river under ground, <tam>பூமியினுள்ளோடுமாறு</tam>. 2. A river in the Congu country, <tam>கொங்குதேசத்தாறு</tam>. <tam>கீழாறுகொண்டுபோயிற்று</tam>. [prov.]</i> An inferior class or fishermen–as distinguished from <tam>மேலோங்கி</tam>, a higher rank.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்நோக்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To look downward, to tend downward, <tam>கீழ்ப்பார்க்க</tam>. 2. To be on the decline–as to wealth, &c.; to go to ruin, to come to naught, <tam>தாழ்வடைய</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்நோக்கித்திட்ட</tam>–<tam>கீழ்நோக்கியேச</tam> <i>inf.</i> To use obscene language, to assail with very indecent speech.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்நோக்கு</tam>–<tam>கீழ்நோக்கம்</tam> <i>v. noun.</i> Looking downward, downward ten- dency, <tam>கீழ்ப்பார்வை</tam>. 2. Low or grovelling pursuits, a base inclination; underhand, clandestine purpose.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்மேலாக</tam>, <i>adv.</i> Upside down.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்பட</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To be subdued, to yield, to be submissive, to become inferior, <tam>கீழ்ப்படிய</tam>. 2. To be subject, to be subor- dinate, to submit to, <tam>அடங்க</tam>. 3. To be degraded, mean, base, <tam>இழிவுபட</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்படிய</tam>–<tam>கீழ்ப்பணிய</tam> <i>inf.</i> To sub- mit, to yield, to obey.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்படியாத்தனம்</tam>–<tam>கீழ்ப்படியாமை</tam>, <i>s.</i> Disobedience, insubordination.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்படிவு</tam>, <i>v. noun.</i> Submission, obe- dience, subordination, subjection, <tam>கீழ்ப்பணிவு</tam>. 2. Docility, tractableness, <tam>அமைவு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்படுத்த</tam>–<tam>கீழ்ப்படியப்பண்ண</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To subdue, to subject, to subordinate, to subjugate, to quell, <tam>அடக்க</tam>. 2. [in astro.]</i> A lunar mansion looking downward–opposed to <tam>மேனோக்கினநட்சத்திரம்</tam>. They are twelve in number. (<tam>உள்ளமு</tam>.)</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்நோக்கினராசி</tam>, <i>s. [in astrol.]</i> A zodiacal sign which looks downward.–<i>Note.</i> These signs, as well as the <tam>கீழ்நோக்கின நட்சத்திரம்</tam>, are favorable for planting esculent roots and digging wells.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்மேற்றென்வடல்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The east, west, north and south.</p2></p> </blockquote>

(See <tam>உலகம்</tam>.) 2. Hell, <tam>நரகம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழோர்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The mean, the vulgar, <tam>கீழ்மக்கள்</tam>. 2. Out-cast, <tam>சண்டாளர்</tam>. <tam>கீழோராயினுந்தாழவுரை</tam>. The lower part of the eye, the part below the pupil, <tam>கண்ணின்கீழ்ப்பக்கம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்க்குரல்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A low tone of voice, <tam>அடிக் குரல்</tam>. 2. <i>[in singing.]</i> Bass, <tam>மந்தவொலி</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்சாதி</tam>–<tam>கீழ்ச்சாதி</tam> <i>s.</i> A low caste, <tam>தாழ்ந்தசாதி</tam>. 2. A person of low origin or obscure birth, <tam>கீழ்ப்பிறப்பு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்த்தரம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> An inferior kind, degree or class; inferiority, <tam>தாழ்வானதரம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்த்தரக்காரன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> An inferior a low person.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்த்தொடை</tam>, <i>s.</i> The lower part of the thigh.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்போகம்</tam>, <i>s. [prov.]</i> Cultivation of edible roots.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்பயிர்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Grain or herbage in the shade or overtopped by another plant; under-plants, <tam>அடிப்பயிர்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்பாடு</tam>, <i>s.</i> The lower side, <tam>கீழ்ப் பக்கம்</tam>. 2. Subordination, inferiority, <tam>அடக்கம்</tam>. <i>(Little used.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்பாறை</tam>, <i>s.</i> A subterranean cell or cavern, <tam>கீழறை</tam>. <i>(Rott.)</i> 2. An under- stratum of rock, <tam>கீழிருக்கும்பாறை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்புறம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The lower side, the under- side, <tam>கீழ்ப்பக்கம்</tam>. 2. The leeward or the leaning side of a vessel, <tam>தாழ்ந்தபக்கம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்மகன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A person of low caste, a mean person, <tam>இழிந்தோன்</tam>. 2. The planet saturn, <tam>சனி</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்மக்கள்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Inferiors, low-caste people, the base, the vulgar, the igno- rant, <tam>இழிந்தோர்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்மாரி</tam>–<tam>கீழ்வாரி</tam>, <i>s.</i> Rain or thunder in the distance, towards the horizon. <tam>கீழ்மாரிகொள்ளுகிறது</tam>. It thunders at a distance.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்மாரிகொண்டுமுழங்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To thun- der near the horizon.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்வயிறு</tam>, <i>s.</i> The lower part of the belly, abdomen, <tam>அடிவயிறு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்க்கதுவாயளபெடை</tam>, <i>s. [in prosody.]</i> One of the eight <tam>அளபெடைத்தொடை</tam>, in which the first letter of every foot in a line, except the penultimate, is prolonged in sound.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்க்கதுவாயியைபு</tam>, <i>s. [in prosody.]</i> A rhyme in which the last letter of every foot of a line, except the second, is the same <tam>ஒரியைபுத்தொடை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்க்கதுவாயெதுகை</tam>, <i>s. [in prosody.]</i> A rhyme or <tam>தொடை</tam>, in which the second letter, of every foot of a line, but the penultimate, is the same, <tam>ஓரெதுகைத்தொடை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்க்கதுவாய்</tam>, <i>s. [in prosody.]</i> Rhyming or <tam>தொடை</tam> in every foot but the penultimate; and in <tam>இயைபுத்தொடை</tam>, in every foot but the second, <tam>கதுவாய்த் தொடையினொன்று</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்க்கதுவாய்முரண்</tam>, <i>s. [in prosody.]</i> A rhyme or <tam>தொடை</tam>, in which the first word in every foot of a line, except the pe- nultimate, has different meanings, <tam>முரண்டொடை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்க்கதுவாய்மோனை</tam>, <i>s. [in prosody.]</i> A rhyme or <tam>தொடை</tam> in which the first letter of every foot of a line, but the penul- timate, is the same, <tam>ஓர்மோனைத்தொடை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்மை</tam>, <i>v. noun.</i> Lowness, meanness, inferiority, baseness, <tam>இழிவு</tam>. 2. Submis- siveness, humbleness, <tam>தாழ்மை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழண்டை</tam>, <i>s. [vul.]</i> East.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழைத்தெரு</tam>, <i>s.</i> The eastern street.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழைப்புறம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The eastern side, part.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ச்சீமை</tam>, <i>s.</i> the eastern country.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்வாடை</tam>, <i>s.</i> The north-east wind.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்விதேகம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The eastern Videha country–one of the nine divisions of the known continent. See <tam>விதேகம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்காய்நெல்லி</tam>, <i>s.</i> A medicinal plant, <tam>கீழாநெல்லி</tam>, Phillanthus niruri.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்பால்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The east, <tam>கிழக்கு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்பூமி</tam>, <i>s.</i> The lower or nether parts of the earth, <tam>பூமியின்கீழ்ப்புறம்</tam>. 2. The nether worlds, <tam>கீழுலகம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்ப்பக்கம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The east side. 2. The underside.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்வாயிலக்கம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Fractional parts or denominations. 2. <i>[modern usage.]</i> De- nominator of a fraction–opposed to <tam>மேல்வாயிலக்கம்</tam>, the numerator.</p2> <p2><tam>கீழ்வாய்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The chin, <tam>மோவாய்</tam>, <tam>சிவுகம்</tam>. 2. <i<[in arithmetic.] Vulgar fractions, fractional parts; sometimes fractional denominations, <tam>கீழ்வாயிலக்கம்</tam>. 3. <i>(local)</i> Pudendum muliebre; posteriors, <tam>கீழ்த்தானம்</tam>.</p2></p> </blockquote>

<script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/jquery-3.2.1.min.js"></script>
<script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/popper.min.js"></script>
<script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/bootstrap.min.js"></script>

<script>

    $(document).ready(function(){
        $(document).keypress(function(event) {
                var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keycode == "116") {
                        var selection = window.getSelection().toString();
			var q_param = $.trim(selection);
			q_param = q_param.replace(/[;]/g, '%3B');
			var q_param = q_param.replace(/\/?#/g,'')
			//console.log(selection)
			//console.log(q_param)
			var q_url = 'tamil/get_transliteration.py?q=' + q_param;
			$.ajax({
				url:q_url,
				dataType: "text"
			}).done(function(data){
				//console.log(data)
				var title_text = selection.replace(/\u00a0\u00a0/g,'\u00a0') 
				title_text = title_text.replace(/\u00a0/g,'<br/>')
				var title = '<span id="transliteration_modal_override">Transliteration for: ' + title_text + '</span>';
				var display_data = '<span id="transliteration_modal_override">' + data + '</span>';
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-title').html(title);
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-body').html(display_data);
				$('#tranliterationModal').modal('show');
			}).fail(function(xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
				console.log(xhr)
				console.log(ajaxOptions)
				console.log(thrownError)
				if (thrownError === 'Request-URI Too Long') {
					var message = "Please select a smaller passage to transliterate";
				}
				else if (thrownError === 'Internal Server Error') {
					var message = "The transliteration code encountered a problem. Please try again.";
				}
				var title = "Error: " + thrownError;
				//var message = "Please select a smaller passage to transliterate";
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-title').text(title);
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-body').text(message);
				$('#tranliterationModal').modal('show');
			});
                };
        });
    });

</script>
